################################
# Eurasianism and Panslavism
################################

event = {
id = 700006
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = { atwar = no }

date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1937 }
offset = 1000
deathdate = { day = 1 month = january year = 1960 }

picture = "russiageo"

name = "Nikolai Trubetskoy Publishes 'Principles of Geopolitics'"
desc = "'Princypiya geopolitiki', published in the late 30's by Nikolai Trubetskoy, is now considered a cornerstone of modern geopolitics. In his book the Russian conservative philosopher and politician envisioned a new Russian Empire. Defined not by the Tsardom or religion but rather by pragmatic control over the Eurasian continent. His ideas were further developed by Lev Gumilov thus creating the so-called Eurasian Doctrine."

action_a = {
	name = "An interesting concept indeed!"
	command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
}
}

country = RUS

	headofstate = 4092 #Aleksandr Kerensky
	government = democratic
}

name = "The Assassination of Kerensky"
desc = "The sound of gunfire rings across the capital. Alexander Kerensky, the President of the Russian Republic was shot and killed by an assassin while he was climbing the steps to the Senate House. His killer was shot dead by the military police before he could make his escape. His motives will forever be unknown. Regardless, the fate of Russia has been irrevocably changed, for better or worse."
picture = "assassinationofker"

date = { day = 5 month = january year = 1936 }
offset = 2
deathdate = { day = 7 month = january year = 1936 }

	name = "A shot that will ring across the world."
	command = { type = sleepminister which = 4092 }
	command = { type = headofstate which = 4280 } # The Senate
	command = { type = event which = 750000 where = RUS when = 1 }
}
}

event = {
id = 758071
random = no
country = RUS

name = "Black Monday hits Russia!"
desc = "Almost three weeks ago the Berlin Stock Exchange plunged into a bottomless depth, throwing Germany's economy into an unprecedented crisis. Now the crash's shockwaves have reached Russia. German and Bohemian-owned companies have closed down or laid off their workers, the Russian ruble is losing value, and resource exports are shrinking."
style = 2
picture = "stockcrashrus"

date = { day = 28 month = february year = 1936 }

action_a = {
	name = "Let's hope the government will save us from the worst!"
	command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = -15 }
	command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	command = { type = money value = -50 }
}
}

		headofstate = 4080 # Kyril Romanov
	}
}

name = "Russian economy"
desc = EVT_759438_DESC
style = 2
picture = "petrogradstockexchange"

date = { day = 16 month = november year = 1936 }
offset = 2
deathdate = { day = 18 month = november year = 1936 }

action_a = {
	ai_chance = 30
	name = "A laissez faire economy has served Tsarist Russia well!"
	command = { type = dissent value = 8 } #socialists, national populists, officers are unhappy with this.
	command = { type = money value = 200 }
	command = { type = setflag which = RUS_FREEMARKET }
	command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = 9 }
}
action_b = {
	ai_chance = 40
	name = "A balanced approach is the best course of action."
	command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
	command = { type = money value = 50 }
	command = { type = setflag which = RUS_BALANCED }
	command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = 1 }
}

	ai_chance = 30
	name = "The Tsar should control the economy!"
	command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	command = { type = setflag which = RUS_STATEECO }
	command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = -3 }
}
}

#################################################################
#Investment in Siberia - Russia controls Vladivostok and Trans-Siberian Railroad
#################################################################
event = {
id = 758033
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = {
	OR = {
		flag = RUS_FREEMARKET
		flag = RUS_BALANCED
	}
	flag = RUS_SIBPEACE #flag which will check if Transamur/Mongolia has submitted/got annexed and does not make any problems for Russia
	flag = RUS_CENASIAPEACE # flag which checks if Kyrgyzstan has gone or Alash Orda has submitted or Russia has annexed both countries
	NOT = { event = 758034 }
}

date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
offset = 600
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1960 }

name = "Investment in Siberia"
desc = "Siberia is once again a stable Russian province, mostly due to the defeat of the Mongols and Transamur. Now we can enact economic policies to develop Siberia and efficiently use its resources without the threat of the Japanese or the Central Asian tribes. Thanks to our pro-capitalist orientation many Russian companies have begun to invest in light and heavy industry in South Siberia and the Urals."

action_a = {
	name = "Great!"
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1162 value = 1 } #Irkutsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1167 value = 1 } #Abakan
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1070 value = 1 } #Krasnoyarsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1190 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1179 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1144 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1138 value = 1 } #Omsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1156 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1132 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1136 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 668 value = 1 } #Kubyszew
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1144 value = 15 where = energy }
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1144 value = 5 where = metal }
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1149 value = 10 where = oil }
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1179 value = 5 where = rare_materials }
	command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
	command = { type = money value = 100 }
}
}

	flag = RUS_STATEECO
	flag = RUS_SIBPEACE #flag which will check if Transamur/Mongolia has submitted/got annexed and does not make any problems for Russia
	flag = RUS_CENASIAPEACE # flag which checks if Kyrgyzstan has gone or Alash Orda has submitted or Russia has annexed both countries
	NOT = { event = 758033 }
}

name = "Investment in Siberia"
desc = "Siberia is once again a stable Russian province, mostly due to the defeat of the Mongols and Transamur. Now we can enact economic policies to develop Siberia and efficiently use its resources without the threat of the Japanese or the Central Asian tribes. Thanks to our pro-centralized orientation our government is able to invest in light and heavy industry in South Siberia and the Urals."

offset = 600
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1960 }

	name = "Great"
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1162 value = 1 } #Irkutsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1167 value = 1 } #Abakan
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1070 value = 1 } #Krasnoyarsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1190 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1179 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1144 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1138 value = 1 } #Omsk
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1156 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1132 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 1136 value = 1 } #
	command = { type = construct which = ic where = 668 value = 1 } #Kubyszew
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1144 value = 15 where = energy }
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1144 value = 5 where = metal }
	command = { type = add_prov_resource which = 1149 value = 10 where = oil }

	command = { type = money value = -80 }

############################
# Post-1936 economic events
############################
# IX Duma economic policies

# Liberal government
event = {
id = 758000
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = {
	headofgovernment = 4160 # Milyukov
	flag = RUS_BALANCED
}

name = "Liberals propose economic reforms"
desc = "After securing a majority in the Duma the Kadet-Liberal coalition has proposed an extensive economic reform project to introduce free market policies in Russia. However, their proposal is opposed not only by the opposition but by the considerable Kadet part of the coalition as well. The present system satisfies the Constitutional Democrats quite well."

date = { day = 1 month = may year = 1937 }
offset = 800
deathdate = { day = 1 month = march year = 1942 }

action_a = {
	ai_chance = 35
	name = "Privatization is essential!"
	command = { type = dissent value = 6 }
	command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = 5 }
	command = { type = setflag which = RUS_FREEMARKET }
	command = { type = clrflag which = RUS_BALANCED }
}
action_b = {
	ai_chance = 65
	name = "The current system suits us fine."
	command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
	command = { type = setflag which = RUS_BALANCED }
}
}


event = {
id = 758001
random = no
country = RUS
style = 2

trigger = {
	headofgovernment = 4160 # Milyukov
	flag = RUS_STATEECO
}

name = "Liberals propose economic reforms"
desc = "After securing a majority in the Duma the Kadet-Liberal coalition has proposed an extensive economic reform project to introduce free market policies in Russia. 		}
	}
}

name = "The Katorga Archipelago"
